[30;1m222 | [0m[35mIn Python 3.7, the `__future__.annotations` feature was introduced ([PEP[0m
[30;1m223 | [0m[35m563](https://peps.python.org/pep-0563/)), which postpones the evaluation of[0m
[30;1m224 | [0m[35mtype annotations.  The effect of this is that *no* type annotations will be[0m
[30;1m225 | [0m[35mevaluated at definition time, and all type annotations will be treated as[0m
